CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "airlineapp_routes" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "codeshare" varchar(1) NOT NULL, "stops" integer NOT NULL, "airline_id_id" bigint NOT NULL REFERENCES "airlineapp_airlines" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "from_airport_id" bigint NOT NULL REFERENCES "airlineapp_airports" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "to_airport_id" bigint NOT NULL REFERENCES "airlineapp_airports" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "auth_user" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "password" varchar(128) NOT NULL, "last_login" datetime NULL, "is_superuser" bool NOT NULL, "username" varchar(150) NOT NULL UNIQUE, "last_name" varchar(150) NOT NULL, "email" varchar(254) NOT NULL, "is_staff" bool NOT NULL, "is_active" bool NOT NULL, "date_joined" datetime NOT NULL, "first_name" varchar(150) NOT NULL);
